Terraform ne détectait pas le changement car la VM existait déjà.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution\u003c/strong\u003e :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUtiliser un tag cohérent \u003ccode\u003e${var.environment}-latest\u003c/code\u003e partout\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAjouter \u003ccode\u003eallow_stopping_for_update = true\u003c/code\u003e dans \u003ccode\u003evm.tf\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEn dernier recours : supprimer la VM pour forcer sa recréation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLeçon apprise\u003c/strong\u003e : Les métadonnées de Container-Optimized OS sont lues au boot. Terraform ne déploie pas les changements de code\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-7-terraform-ne-déploie-pas-les-changements-de-code\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 7. Terraform ne déploie pas les changements de code\" href=\"#7-terraform-ne-déploie-pas-les-changements-de-code\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eProblème\u003c/strong\u003e : Après un push de nouvelles modifications de code (v1.1), la VM GCP continue d'exécuter l'ancienne version. Terraform dit \"No changes\" alors que le code a changé.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCause racine\u003c/strong\u003e : Terraform gère l'\u003cstrong\u003einfrastructure\u003c/strong\u003e, pas le \u003cstrong\u003econtenu\u003c/strong\u003e des images Docker.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVoici ce que Terraform voit :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-hcl notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# vm.tf - métadonnées du container\ncontainer_image = \u0026quot;gcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e vm.tf - métadonnées du container\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003econtainer_image\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003egcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTerraform compare la \u003cstrong\u003econfiguration\u003c/strong\u003e (le tag de l'image), pas le \u003cstrong\u003econtenu\u003c/strong\u003e de l'image. Puisque le tag reste \u003ccode\u003edev-latest\u003c/code\u003e, Terraform ne détecte aucun changement.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCe qui se passe en réalité\u003c/strong\u003e :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGitHub Actions build une nouvelle image Docker avec le nouveau code\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGitHub Actions pousse l'image sur GCR avec le tag \u003ccode\u003edev-latest\u003c/code\u003e (écrase l'ancienne)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTerraform compare : \u003ccode\u003edev-latest\u003c/code\u003e == \u003ccode\u003edev-latest\u003c/code\u003e → \u003cstrong\u003eAucun changement\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLa VM garde son ancienne image en cache → \u003cstrong\u003eL'ancien code continue de tourner\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePourquoi c'est contre-intuitif\u003c/strong\u003e :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLe tag \u003ccode\u003e:dev-latest\u003c/code\u003e pointe vers une nouvelle image dans GCR\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMais la VM a déjà téléchargé l'ancienne image et ne la re-télécharge pas\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eContainer-Optimized OS ne pull pas automatiquement les nouvelles images\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolutions possibles\u003c/strong\u003e :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eSolution\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eAvantage\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eInconvénient\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003egcloud compute instances reset\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eSimple, reboot complet\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eDowntime ~60s\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003ccode\u003egcloud compute instances update-container\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003ePas de reboot, rapide\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eRedémarre le container\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eTags uniques (ex: \u003ccode\u003edev-abc123\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eTerraform détecte le changement\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eComplexifie la gestion des tags\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAjouter un hash dans les métadonnées\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eForce la mise à jour\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eWorkaround un peu \"hacky\"\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution implémentée\u003c/strong\u003e : Workflow GitHub Actions intelligent qui détecte si l'infra change :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# .github/workflows/deploy.yml\n- name: Terraform Plan\n  run: |\n    terraform plan -detailed-exitcode -out=tfplan || exit_code=$?\n    # Exit code 0 = no changes, 1 = error, 2 = changes\n    if [ \u0026quot;${exit_code:-0}\u0026quot; -eq 2 ]; then\n      echo \u0026quot;has_changes=true\u0026quot; \u0026gt;\u0026gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT\n    else\n      echo \u0026quot;has_changes=false\u0026quot; \u0026gt;\u0026gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT\n    fi\n\n- name: Terraform Apply\n  if: steps.plan.outputs.has_changes == 'true'\n data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Post-Mortem : Mini Terraform - Station Météo</h1><a id="user-content-post-mortem--mini-terraform---station-météo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Post-Mortem : Mini Terraform - Station Météo" href="#post-mortem--mini-terraform---station-météo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contexte du projet</h2><a id="user-content-contexte-du-projet" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contexte du projet" href="#contexte-du-projet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Objectif</strong> : Déployer une application Django sur GCP via Terraform et GitHub Actions, avec 3 environnements (dev, staging, prod).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Durée du développement</strong> : ~2 sessions de travail</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Technologies</strong> : Django 5.0, Python 3.12, Terraform, GCP (Compute Engine, Cloud Storage), Docker, GitHub Actions</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Chronologie des difficultés et solutions</h2><a id="user-content-chronologie-des-difficultés-et-solutions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Chronologie des difficultés et solutions" href="#chronologie-des-difficultés-et-solutions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Authentification GCR/Artifact Registry</h3><a id="user-content-1-authentification-gcrartifact-registry" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Authentification GCR/Artifact Registry" href="#1-authentification-gcrartifact-registry"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : La VM ne pouvait pas pull l'image Docker depuis Google Container Registry.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="denied: Unauthenticated request... do not have permission artifactregistry.repositories.downloadArtifacts"><pre class="notranslate"><code>denied: Unauthenticated request... do not have permission artifactregistry.repositories.downloadArtifacts
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : Google a migré GCR vers Artifact Registry en 2023. Le service account de la VM n'avait que <code>storage.objectViewer</code>, insuffisant pour la nouvelle API.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution</strong> : Ajouter deux rôles IAM au service account de la VM :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-hcl notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# iam.tf
resource &quot;google_project_iam_member&quot; &quot;vm_gcr_reader&quot; {
  role   = &quot;roles/storage.objectViewer&quot;
  member = &quot;serviceAccount:${google_service_account.vm_sa.email}&quot;
}

resource &quot;google_project_iam_member&quot; &quot;vm_artifact_reader&quot; {
  role   = &quot;roles/artifactregistry.reader&quot;
  member = &quot;serviceAccount:${google_service_account.vm_sa.email}&quot;
}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> iam.tf<span class="pl-c"></span></span>
<span class="pl-en">resource</span> <span class="pl-smi">"google_project_iam_member"</span> <span class="pl-smi">"vm_gcr_reader"</span> {
  <span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">role</span>   <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>roles/storage.objectViewer<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">member</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>serviceAccount:<span class="pl-k">${</span><span class="pl-smi">google_service_account</span><span class="pl-k">.</span><span class="pl-smi">vm_sa</span><span class="pl-k">.</span><span class="pl-smi">email</span><span class="pl-k">}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}

<span class="pl-en">resource</span> <span class="pl-smi">"google_project_iam_member"</span> <span class="pl-smi">"vm_artifact_reader"</span> {
  <span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">role</span>   <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>roles/artifactregistry.reader<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">member</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>serviceAccount:<span class="pl-k">${</span><span class="pl-smi">google_service_account</span><span class="pl-k">.</span><span class="pl-smi">vm_sa</span><span class="pl-k">.</span><span class="pl-smi">email</span><span class="pl-k">}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Les migrations de services GCP peuvent casser silencieusement des configurations existantes. Toujours vérifier la documentation officielle pour les changements récents.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Tag d'image Docker incorrect</h3><a id="user-content-2-tag-dimage-docker-incorrect" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Tag d'image Docker incorrect" href="#2-tag-dimage-docker-incorrect"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : La VM tentait de pull <code>gcr.io/project/meteo-app:latest</code> alors que le workflow poussait <code>gcr.io/project/meteo-app:dev-latest</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : Incohérence entre le tag dans le workflow GitHub Actions et les métadonnées de la VM Terraform. Terraform ne détectait pas le changement car la VM existait déjà.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution</strong> :</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Utiliser un tag cohérent <code>${var.environment}-latest</code> partout</li>
<li>Ajouter <code>allow_stopping_for_update = true</code> dans <code>vm.tf</code></li>
<li>En dernier recours : supprimer la VM pour forcer sa recréation</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Les métadonnées de Container-Optimized OS sont lues au boot. Un changement de tag nécessite soit un reboot, soit une recréation de la VM.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE non configuré</h3><a id="user-content-3-django_settings_module-non-configuré" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE non configuré" href="#3-django_settings_module-non-configuré"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : Erreur 500 sur <code>/graph/</code> avec le message :</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Requested setting GCP_PROJECT_ID, but settings are not configured.
You must either define the environment variable DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Requested setting GCP_PROJECT_ID, but settings are not configured.
You must either define the environment variable DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : La variable <code>DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE</code> n'était pas passée au conteneur dans les métadonnées de la VM.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Pourquoi c'est piégeux</strong> :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Gunicorn démarre correctement sans cette variable</li>
<li>L'erreur n'apparaît que quand une vue accède à <code>django.conf.settings</code></li>
<li>Le serveur semble fonctionner, mais certaines pages crashent</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution</strong> : Ajouter la variable dans les métadonnées du conteneur :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-hcl notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# vm.tf - dans gce-container-declaration
env = [
  { name = &quot;GCS_BUCKET_NAME&quot;, value = var.bucket_name },
  { name = &quot;GCP_PROJECT_ID&quot;, value = var.project_id },
  { name = &quot;DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE&quot;, value = &quot;meteo.settings&quot; },  # &lt;-- Crucial
  { name = &quot;DEBUG&quot;, value = var.environment == &quot;dev&quot; ? &quot;true&quot; : &quot;false&quot; }
]"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> vm.tf - dans gce-container-declaration<span class="pl-c"></span></span>
<span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">env</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span>[
  { name <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GCS_BUCKET_NAME<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, value <span class="pl-k">=</span> var.bucket_name },
  { name <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>GCP_PROJECT_ID<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, value <span class="pl-k">=</span> var.project_id },
  { name <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, value <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>meteo.settings<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> },  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> &lt;-- Crucial<span class="pl-c"></span></span>
  { name <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DEBUG<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, value <span class="pl-k">=</span> var.environment <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>dev<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>false<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> }
]</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Toujours tester toutes les routes de l'application, pas seulement la page d'accueil. Django lazy-load ses settings.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Compatibilité des styles Matplotlib</h3><a id="user-content-4-compatibilité-des-styles-matplotlib" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Compatibilité des styles Matplotlib" href="#4-compatibilité-des-styles-matplotlib"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : Erreur lors de la génération des graphiques :</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="OSError: 'seaborn-whitegrid' is not a valid style"><pre class="notranslate"><code>OSError: 'seaborn-whitegrid' is not a valid style
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : Les noms des styles Matplotlib ont changé entre versions :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Matplotlib &lt; 3.6 : <code>seaborn-whitegrid</code></li>
<li>Matplotlib &gt;= 3.6 : <code>seaborn-v0_8-whitegrid</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution</strong> : Implémenter un système de fallback :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="try:
    plt.style.use('seaborn-v0_8-whitegrid')
except OSError:
    try:
        plt.style.use('seaborn-whitegrid')
    except OSError:
        plt.style.use('ggplot')  # Fallback universel"><pre><span class="pl-k">try</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-c1">style</span>.<span class="pl-c1">use</span>(<span class="pl-s">'seaborn-v0_8-whitegrid'</span>)
<span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">OSError</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-c1">style</span>.<span class="pl-c1">use</span>(<span class="pl-s">'seaborn-whitegrid'</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">OSError</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-c1">style</span>.<span class="pl-c1">use</span>(<span class="pl-s">'ggplot'</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># Fallback universel</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Les dépendances peuvent changer de comportement entre versions mineures. Toujours prévoir des fallbacks pour les fonctionnalités non critiques.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. IndexError dans resample_hourly()</h3><a id="user-content-5-indexerror-dans-resample_hourly" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. IndexError dans resample_hourly()" href="#5-indexerror-dans-resample_hourly"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : Erreur 500 lors de l'affichage des graphiques :</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="IndexError: list index out of range"><pre class="notranslate"><code>IndexError: list index out of range
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : Le parsing des données météo pouvait échouer sur certaines lignes (données corrompues, format invalide), créant des listes de longueurs différentes dans le dictionnaire <code>data</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Avant : crash si data['temp_out'] a moins d'éléments que data['dates']
for i, dt in enumerate(data['dates']):
    hourly[hour_key]['temp_out'].append(data['temp_out'][i])  # IndexError!"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Avant : crash si data['temp_out'] a moins d'éléments que data['dates']</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dt</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data</span>[<span class="pl-s">'dates'</span>]):
    <span class="pl-s1">hourly</span>[<span class="pl-s1">hour_key</span>][<span class="pl-s">'temp_out'</span>].<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data</span>[<span class="pl-s">'temp_out'</span>][<span class="pl-s1">i</span>])  <span class="pl-c"># IndexError!</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution</strong> : Vérifier les indices avant accès :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="for i, dt in enumerate(data['dates']):
    for key in data:
        if key == 'dates':
            continue
        if i &lt; len(data[key]):  # &lt;-- Vérification ajoutée
            hourly[hour_key][key].append(data[key][i])"><pre><span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dt</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data</span>[<span class="pl-s">'dates'</span>]):
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'dates'</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">continue</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data</span>[<span class="pl-s1">key</span>]):  <span class="pl-c"># &lt;-- Vérification ajoutée</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">hourly</span>[<span class="pl-s1">hour_key</span>][<span class="pl-s1">key</span>].<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data</span>[<span class="pl-s1">key</span>][<span class="pl-s1">i</span>])</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Les données externes sont imprévisibles. Toujours valider les indices et gérer les cas où les données sont incomplètes.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Configuration par environnement (local vs GCP)</h3><a id="user-content-6-configuration-par-environnement-local-vs-gcp" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. Configuration par environnement (local vs GCP)" href="#6-configuration-par-environnement-local-vs-gcp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : Comment exécuter le même code en local (sans GCP) et sur GCP (avec GCS) ?</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution initiale envisagée</strong> : Modifier le code pour chaque environnement (mauvaise pratique).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution implémentée</strong> : Architecture dual-mode avec variables d'environnement :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# settings.py
STORAGE_MODE = os.environ.get(&quot;STORAGE_MODE&quot;, &quot;gcs&quot;)  # &quot;local&quot; ou &quot;gcs&quot;
LOCAL_DATA_DIR = os.environ.get(&quot;LOCAL_DATA_DIR&quot;, &quot;/tmp&quot;)

# views.py
def is_local_mode() -&gt; bool:
    return settings.STORAGE_MODE == &quot;local&quot;

def download_from_storage() -&gt; str | None:
    if is_local_mode():
        # Lecture depuis le filesystem
        return Path(settings.LOCAL_DATA_DIR).joinpath(BLOB_NAME).read_text()
    else:
        # Lecture depuis GCS
        from google.cloud import storage  # Import conditionnel
        client = storage.Client()
        return client.bucket(settings.GCS_BUCKET_NAME).blob(BLOB_NAME).download_as_text()"><pre><span class="pl-c"># settings.py</span>
<span class="pl-c1">STORAGE_MODE</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">environ</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"STORAGE_MODE"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"gcs"</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># "local" ou "gcs"</span>
<span class="pl-c1">LOCAL_DATA_DIR</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">environ</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"LOCAL_DATA_DIR"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"/tmp"</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># views.py</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">is_local_mode</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">bool</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">settings</span>.<span class="pl-c1">STORAGE_MODE</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"local"</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">download_from_storage</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">is_local_mode</span>():
        <span class="pl-c"># Lecture depuis le filesystem</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s1">settings</span>.<span class="pl-c1">LOCAL_DATA_DIR</span>).<span class="pl-c1">joinpath</span>(<span class="pl-c1">BLOB_NAME</span>).<span class="pl-c1">read_text</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Lecture depuis GCS</span>
        <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">google</span>.<span class="pl-s1">cloud</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">storage</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Import conditionnel</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">storage</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Client</span>()
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-c1">bucket</span>(<span class="pl-s1">settings</span>.<span class="pl-c1">GCS_BUCKET_NAME</span>).<span class="pl-c1">blob</span>(<span class="pl-c1">BLOB_NAME</span>).<span class="pl-c1">download_as_text</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Points clés</strong> :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Import de <code>google.cloud.storage</code> à l'intérieur de la fonction pour éviter <code>ImportError</code> en local</li>
<li>Même code, comportement différent selon les variables d'environnement</li>
<li>Fichier <code>.env.example</code> pour documenter les variables</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Le pattern "configuration by environment" est la bonne pratique. Le code ne doit jamais changer entre environnements, seule la configuration change.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bonnes pratiques identifiées</h2><a id="user-content-bonnes-pratiques-identifiées" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bonnes pratiques identifiées" href="#bonnes-pratiques-identifiées"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Infrastructure as Code (Terraform)</h3><a id="user-content-infrastructure-as-code-terraform" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Infrastructure as Code (Terraform)" href="#infrastructure-as-code-terraform"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>State distant</strong> : Toujours stocker le state dans un bucket GCS, jamais en local</li>
<li><strong>Isolation</strong> : Un state par environnement (<code>terraform/state/dev/</code>, <code>staging/</code>, <code>prod/</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Variables</strong> : Utiliser des variables pour tout ce qui change entre environnements</li>
<li><strong>Depends_on</strong> : Expliciter les dépendances entre ressources</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CI/CD (GitHub Actions)</h3><a id="user-content-cicd-github-actions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CI/CD (GitHub Actions)" href="#cicd-github-actions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Secrets</strong> : Ne jamais commiter de credentials, utiliser GitHub Secrets</li>
<li><strong>Environnement automatique</strong> : Déduire l'environnement de la branche (<code>dev</code>, <code>staging</code>, <code>prod</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Summary</strong> : Afficher les outputs importants (IP, URL) dans le Job Summary</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Django/Python</h3><a id="user-content-djangopython" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Django/Python" href="#djangopython"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Settings depuis l'environnement</strong> : <code>os.environ.get()</code> avec valeurs par défaut</li>
<li><strong>Gestion d'erreurs</strong> : Capturer les exceptions et afficher des messages utiles</li>
<li><strong>Fallbacks</strong> : Prévoir des alternatives quand une fonctionnalité peut échouer</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Docker</h3><a id="user-content-docker" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docker" href="#docker"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Variables d'environnement</strong> : Passer la config via <code>-e</code> ou <code>env</code> dans les métadonnées</li>
<li><strong>Tags cohérents</strong> : Utiliser le même schéma de tags partout</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Métriques du projet</h2><a id="user-content-métriques-du-projet" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Métriques du projet" href="#métriques-du-projet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7. Terraform ne déploie pas les changements de code</h3><a id="user-content-7-terraform-ne-déploie-pas-les-changements-de-code" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7. Terraform ne déploie pas les changements de code" href="#7-terraform-ne-déploie-pas-les-changements-de-code"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problème</strong> : Après un push de nouvelles modifications de code (v1.1), la VM GCP continue d'exécuter l'ancienne version. Terraform dit "No changes" alors que le code a changé.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Cause racine</strong> : Terraform gère l'<strong>infrastructure</strong>, pas le <strong>contenu</strong> des images Docker.</p>
<p dir="auto">Voici ce que Terraform voit :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-hcl notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# vm.tf - métadonnées du container
container_image = &quot;gcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> vm.tf - métadonnées du container<span class="pl-c"></span></span>
<span class="pl-v"><span class="pl-smi">container_image</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> </span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Terraform compare la <strong>configuration</strong> (le tag de l'image), pas le <strong>contenu</strong> de l'image. Puisque le tag reste <code>dev-latest</code>, Terraform ne détecte aucun changement.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Ce qui se passe en réalité</strong> :</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>GitHub Actions build une nouvelle image Docker avec le nouveau code</li>
<li>GitHub Actions pousse l'image sur GCR avec le tag <code>dev-latest</code> (écrase l'ancienne)</li>
<li>Terraform compare : <code>dev-latest</code> == <code>dev-latest</code> → <strong>Aucun changement</strong></li>
<li>La VM garde son ancienne image en cache → <strong>L'ancien code continue de tourner</strong></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Pourquoi c'est contre-intuitif</strong> :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Le tag <code>:dev-latest</code> pointe vers une nouvelle image dans GCR</li>
<li>Mais la VM a déjà téléchargé l'ancienne image et ne la re-télécharge pas</li>
<li>Container-Optimized OS ne pull pas automatiquement les nouvelles images</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions possibles</strong> :</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Solution</th>
<th>Avantage</th>
<th>Inconvénient</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>gcloud compute instances reset</code></td>
<td>Simple, reboot complet</td>
<td>Downtime ~60s</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>gcloud compute instances update-container</code></td>
<td>Pas de reboot, rapide</td>
<td>Redémarre le container</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tags uniques (ex: <code>dev-abc123</code>)</td>
<td>Terraform détecte le changement</td>
<td>Complexifie la gestion des tags</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ajouter un hash dans les métadonnées</td>
<td>Force la mise à jour</td>
<td>Workaround un peu "hacky"</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution implémentée</strong> : Workflow GitHub Actions intelligent qui détecte si l'infra change :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# .github/workflows/deploy.yml
- name: Terraform Plan
  run: |
    terraform plan -detailed-exitcode -out=tfplan || exit_code=$?
    # Exit code 0 = no changes, 1 = error, 2 = changes
    if [ &quot;${exit_code:-0}&quot; -eq 2 ]; then
      echo &quot;has_changes=true&quot; &gt;&gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT
    else
      echo &quot;has_changes=false&quot; &gt;&gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT
    fi

- name: Terraform Apply
  if: steps.plan.outputs.has_changes == 'true'
  run: terraform apply -auto-approve tfplan

# Job séparé si pas de changement d'infra
restart-vm:
  if: needs.terraform.outputs.has_changes == 'false'
  steps:
    - name: Restart VM to pull new Docker image
      run: gcloud compute instances reset ${VM_NAME} --zone=${ZONE}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> .github/workflows/deploy.yml</span>
- <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">Terraform Plan</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">run</span>: <span class="pl-s">|</span>
<span class="pl-s">    terraform plan -detailed-exitcode -out=tfplan || exit_code=$?</span>
<span class="pl-s">    # Exit code 0 = no changes, 1 = error, 2 = changes</span>
<span class="pl-s">    if [ "${exit_code:-0}" -eq 2 ]; then</span>
<span class="pl-s">      echo "has_changes=true" &gt;&gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT</span>
<span class="pl-s">    else</span>
<span class="pl-s">      echo "has_changes=false" &gt;&gt; $GITHUB_OUTPUT</span>
<span class="pl-s">    fi</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>- <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">Terraform Apply</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">if</span>: <span class="pl-s">steps.plan.outputs.has_changes == 'true'</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">run</span>: <span class="pl-s">terraform apply -auto-approve tfplan</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Job séparé si pas de changement d'infra</span>
<span class="pl-ent">restart-vm</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">if</span>: <span class="pl-s">needs.terraform.outputs.has_changes == 'false'</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">steps</span>:
    - <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">Restart VM to pull new Docker image</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">run</span>: <span class="pl-s">gcloud compute instances reset ${VM_NAME} --zone=${ZONE}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Le flag <code>-detailed-exitcode</code></strong> :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Exit code <code>0</code> : Aucun changement d'infrastructure</li>
<li>Exit code <code>1</code> : Erreur</li>
<li>Exit code <code>2</code> : Des changements sont détectés</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Commande alternative sans reboot</strong> :</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gcloud compute instances update-container meteo-vm-dev \
  --zone=europe-west1-b \
  --container-image=gcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest"><pre>gcloud compute instances update-container meteo-vm-dev \
  --zone=europe-west1-b \
  --container-image=gcr.io/mini-terraform/meteo-app:dev-latest</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Cette commande met à jour les métadonnées et redémarre uniquement le container, sans rebooter la VM entière.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Leçon apprise</strong> : Terraform est un outil d'<strong>Infrastructure as Code</strong>, pas de déploiement continu. Pour les changements de code applicatif, il faut un mécanisme complémentaire (restart, rolling update, ou utiliser un orchestrateur comme Kubernetes).</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Améliorations futures possibles</h2><a id="user-content-améliorations-futures-possibles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Améliorations futures possibles" href="#améliorations-futures-possibles"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>HTTPS</strong> : Ajouter un certificat SSL (Let's Encrypt + load balancer ou Cloud Run)</li>
<li><strong>Monitoring</strong> : Intégrer Cloud Monitoring pour les alertes</li>
<li><strong>Tests</strong> : Ajouter des tests unitaires et d'intégration</li>
<li><strong>Cache</strong> : Mettre en cache les graphiques pour éviter de les régénérer à chaque requête</li>
<li><strong>Scheduled refresh</strong> : Cloud Scheduler pour actualiser les données automatiquement</li>
<li><strong>IP statique</strong> : Réserver une IP pour éviter qu'elle change à chaque redéploiement</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conclusion</h2><a id="user-content-conclusion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conclusion" href="#conclusion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ce projet illustre bien la complexité "cachée" du déploiement cloud :</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>La logique métier (Django/Matplotlib) représente ~20% du travail</li>
<li>L'infrastructure et le déploiement (Terraform/GCP/Docker/CI-CD) représentent ~80%</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Les principales sources de bugs étaient :</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Incohérences de configuration</strong> entre différentes parties du système</li>
<li><strong>Changements de comportement</strong> des services cloud (migration GCR → Artifact Registry)</li>
<li><strong>Données externes imprévisibles</strong> (format des données météo)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">La clé du succès : <strong>tester en local avant de déployer</strong>, et <strong>avoir des logs détaillés</strong> pour diagnostiquer les problèmes en production.</p>
</article></div><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div><div class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 kuJVuq"></div><div class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 iafbuG Panel-module__Box--lC3LD panel-content-narrow-styles
